0                                  18878              *
                                   18879              *    On entry:
                                   18880              *      R1  -  Points to the SHOW DSNAMES work area,
                                   18881              *             which contains the page array and options
                                   18882              *
                                   18883              *             The first halfword on each page is the total
                                   18884              *             number of bytes of information on that page.
                                   18885              *             Each line on the page is preceded by a byte
                                   18886              *             which indicates the line length. A zero byte
                                   18887              *             indicates all done.

                                   18889              *    Note: This routine does not return to its caller.

0                                  23185              *
                                   23186              *    This routine is called by the DSPCAT subroutine to get the
                                   23187              *    next line for display.
                                   23188              *
                                   23189              *    On entry:
                                   23190              *      R1  -  Points to the SHOW CATALOG work area which
                                   23191              *             contains a work area used by this routine.
                                   23192              *
                                   23193              *      PAR -  Points to the current page being displayed.
                                   23194              *
                                   23195              *    On output:
                                   23196              *      R0,R1 - describe the length and location of the retrieved
                                   23197              *              line
                                   23198              *      R15=0   means a line was retrieved
                                   23199              *         =NZ  means EOF (no more lines in the display).
                                   23200              *
